By eliminating Player 4, we reduce the villagers' credibility and can possibly cast suspicion on other players in subsequent rounds.

I choose to kill Player 3. My reason is: Player 3 is universally believed to be a villager by all remaining players that are alive, all assigning a probability of 1.0 to their innocence, making them a credible threat to werewolf anonymity. Additionally, given that there is no clear indication of the Seer's identity, there is a risk that Player 3 could be the Seer, given their perceived trustworthiness amongst other villagers. Eliminating this player could reduce the informational advantage of the villagers and sow further confusion, aiding in our deception as the remaining werewolves.
